\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{1 \textcolor{comment}{/* stb\_image -\/ v2.14 -\/ public domain image loader -\/ http://nothings.org/stb\_image.h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2 \textcolor{comment}{no warranty implied; use at your own risk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3 \textcolor{comment}{Do this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4 \textcolor{comment}{\#define STB\_IMAGE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5 \textcolor{comment}{before you include this file in *one* C or C++ file to create the implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6 \textcolor{comment}{// i.e. it should look like this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7 \textcolor{comment}{\#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8 \textcolor{comment}{\#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{9 \textcolor{comment}{\#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{10 \textcolor{comment}{\#define STB\_IMAGE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{11 \textcolor{comment}{\#include "{}stb\_image.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{12 \textcolor{comment}{You can \#define STBI\_ASSERT(x) before the \#include to avoid using assert.h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{13 \textcolor{comment}{And \#define STBI\_MALLOC, STBI\_REALLOC, and STBI\_FREE to avoid using malloc,realloc,free}}
\DoxyCodeLine{14 \textcolor{comment}{QUICK NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{15 \textcolor{comment}{Primarily of interest to game developers and other people who can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{16 \textcolor{comment}{avoid problematic images and only need the trivial interface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{17 \textcolor{comment}{JPEG baseline \& progressive (12 bpc/arithmetic not supported, same as stock IJG lib)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{18 \textcolor{comment}{PNG 1/2/4/8-\/bit-\/per-\/channel (16 bpc not supported)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{19 \textcolor{comment}{TGA (not sure what subset, if a subset)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{20 \textcolor{comment}{BMP non-\/1bpp, non-\/RLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{21 \textcolor{comment}{PSD (composited view only, no extra channels, 8/16 bit-\/per-\/channel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{22 \textcolor{comment}{GIF (*comp always reports as 4-\/channel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{23 \textcolor{comment}{HDR (radiance rgbE format)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{24 \textcolor{comment}{PIC (Softimage PIC)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{25 \textcolor{comment}{PNM (PPM and PGM binary only)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{26 \textcolor{comment}{Animated GIF still needs a proper API, but here's one way to do it:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{27 \textcolor{comment}{http://gist.github.com/urraka/685d9a6340b26b830d49}}
\DoxyCodeLine{28 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ decode from memory or through FILE (define STBI\_NO\_STDIO to remove code)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{29 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ decode from arbitrary I/O callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{30 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ SIMD acceleration on x86/x64 (SSE2) and ARM (NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{31 \textcolor{comment}{Full documentation under "{}DOCUMENTATION"{} below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{32 \textcolor{comment}{Revision 2.00 release notes:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{33 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ Progressive JPEG is now supported.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{34 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ PPM and PGM binary formats are now supported, thanks to Ken Miller.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{35 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ x86 platforms now make use of SSE2 SIMD instructions for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{36 \textcolor{comment}{JPEG decoding, and ARM platforms can use NEON SIMD if requested.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{37 \textcolor{comment}{This work was done by Fabian "{}ryg"{} Giesen. SSE2 is used by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{38 \textcolor{comment}{default, but NEON must be enabled explicitly; see docs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{39 \textcolor{comment}{With other JPEG optimizations included in this version, we see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{40 \textcolor{comment}{2x speedup on a JPEG on an x86 machine, and a 1.5x speedup}}
\DoxyCodeLine{41 \textcolor{comment}{on a JPEG on an ARM machine, relative to previous versions of this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{42 \textcolor{comment}{library. The same results will not obtain for all JPGs and for all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{43 \textcolor{comment}{x86/ARM machines. (Note that progressive JPEGs are significantly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{44 \textcolor{comment}{slower to decode than regular JPEGs.) This doesn't mean that this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{45 \textcolor{comment}{is the fastest JPEG decoder in the land; rather, it brings it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{46 \textcolor{comment}{closer to parity with standard libraries. If you want the fastest}}
\DoxyCodeLine{47 \textcolor{comment}{decode, look elsewhere. (See "{}Philosophy"{} section of docs below.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{48 \textcolor{comment}{See final bullet items below for more info on SIMD.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{49 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ Added STBI\_MALLOC, STBI\_REALLOC, and STBI\_FREE macros for replacing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{50 \textcolor{comment}{the memory allocator. Unlike other STBI libraries, these macros don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{51 \textcolor{comment}{support a context parameter, so if you need to pass a context in to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{52 \textcolor{comment}{the allocator, you'll have to store it in a global or a thread-\/local}}
\DoxyCodeLine{53 \textcolor{comment}{variable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{54 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ Split existing STBI\_NO\_HDR flag into two flags, STBI\_NO\_HDR and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{55 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_LINEAR.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{56 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_HDR:     suppress implementation of .hdr reader format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{57 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_LINEAR:  suppress high-\/dynamic-\/range light-\/linear float API}}
\DoxyCodeLine{58 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ You can suppress implementation of any of the decoders to reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{59 \textcolor{comment}{your code footprint by \#defining one or more of the following}}
\DoxyCodeLine{60 \textcolor{comment}{symbols before creating the implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{61 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{62 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{63 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{64 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{65 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_TGA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{66 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_GIF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{67 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_HDR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{68 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_PIC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{69 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_NO\_PNM   (.ppm and .pgm)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{70 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ You can request *only* certain decoders and suppress all other ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{71 \textcolor{comment}{(this will be more forward-\/compatible, as addition of new decoders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{72 \textcolor{comment}{doesn't require you to disable them explicitly):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{73 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{74 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{75 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{76 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{77 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_TGA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{78 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_GIF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{79 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_HDR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{80 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_PIC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{81 \textcolor{comment}{STBI\_ONLY\_PNM   (.ppm and .pgm)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{82 \textcolor{comment}{Note that you can define multiples of these, and you will get all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{83 \textcolor{comment}{of them ("{}only x"{} and "{}only y"{} is interpreted to mean "{}only x\&y"{}).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{84 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ If you use STBI\_NO\_PNG (or \_ONLY\_ without PNG), and you still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{85 \textcolor{comment}{want the zlib decoder to be available, \#define STBI\_SUPPORT\_ZLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{86 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ Compilation of all SIMD code can be suppressed with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{87 \textcolor{comment}{\#define STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{88 \textcolor{comment}{It should not be necessary to disable SIMD unless you have issues}}
\DoxyCodeLine{89 \textcolor{comment}{compiling (e.g. using an x86 compiler which doesn't support SSE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{90 \textcolor{comment}{intrinsics or that doesn't support the method used to detect}}
\DoxyCodeLine{91 \textcolor{comment}{SSE2 support at run-\/time), and even those can be reported as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{92 \textcolor{comment}{bugs so I can refine the built-\/in compile-\/time checking to be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{93 \textcolor{comment}{smarter.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{94 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ The old STBI\_SIMD system which allowed installing a user-\/defined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{95 \textcolor{comment}{IDCT etc. has been removed. If you need this, don't upgrade. My}}
\DoxyCodeLine{96 \textcolor{comment}{assumption is that almost nobody was doing this, and those who}}
\DoxyCodeLine{97 \textcolor{comment}{were will find the built-\/in SIMD more satisfactory anyway.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{98 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ RGB values computed for JPEG images are slightly different from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{99 \textcolor{comment}{previous versions of stb\_image. (This is due to using less}}
\DoxyCodeLine{100 \textcolor{comment}{integer precision in SIMD.) The C code has been adjusted so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{101 \textcolor{comment}{that the same RGB values will be computed regardless of whether}}
\DoxyCodeLine{102 \textcolor{comment}{SIMD support is available, so your app should always produce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{103 \textcolor{comment}{consistent results. But these results are slightly different from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{104 \textcolor{comment}{previous versions. (Specifically, about 3\% of available YCbCr values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{105 \textcolor{comment}{will compute different RGB results from pre-\/1.49 versions by +-\/1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{106 \textcolor{comment}{most of the deviating values are one smaller in the G channel.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{107 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ If you must produce consistent results with previous versions of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{108 \textcolor{comment}{stb\_image, \#define STBI\_JPEG\_OLD and you will get the same results}}
\DoxyCodeLine{109 \textcolor{comment}{you used to; however, you will not get the SIMD speedups for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{110 \textcolor{comment}{the YCbCr-\/to-\/RGB conversion step (although you should still see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{111 \textcolor{comment}{significant JPEG speedup from the other changes).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{112 \textcolor{comment}{Please note that STBI\_JPEG\_OLD is a temporary feature; it will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{113 \textcolor{comment}{removed in future versions of the library. It is only intended for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{114 \textcolor{comment}{near-\/term back-\/compatibility use.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{115 \textcolor{comment}{Latest revision history:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{116 \textcolor{comment}{2.13  (2016-\/12-\/04) experimental 16-\/bit API, only for PNG so far; fixes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{117 \textcolor{comment}{2.12  (2016-\/04-\/02) fix typo in 2.11 PSD fix that caused crashes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{118 \textcolor{comment}{2.11  (2016-\/04-\/02) 16-\/bit PNGS; enable SSE2 in non-\/gcc x64}}
\DoxyCodeLine{119 \textcolor{comment}{RGB-\/format JPEG; remove white matting in PSD;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{120 \textcolor{comment}{allocate large structures on the stack;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{121 \textcolor{comment}{correct channel count for PNG \& BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{122 \textcolor{comment}{2.10  (2016-\/01-\/22) avoid warning introduced in 2.09}}
\DoxyCodeLine{123 \textcolor{comment}{2.09  (2016-\/01-\/16) 16-\/bit TGA; comments in PNM files; STBI\_REALLOC\_SIZED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{124 \textcolor{comment}{2.08  (2015-\/09-\/13) fix to 2.07 cleanup, reading RGB PSD as RGBA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{125 \textcolor{comment}{2.07  (2015-\/09-\/13) partial animated GIF support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{126 \textcolor{comment}{limited 16-\/bit PSD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{127 \textcolor{comment}{minor bugs, code cleanup, and compiler warnings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{128 \textcolor{comment}{See end of file for full revision history.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{167 \textcolor{comment}{// DOCUMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{168 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{169 \textcolor{comment}{// Limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{170 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no 16-\/bit-\/per-\/channel PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{171 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no 12-\/bit-\/per-\/channel JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{172 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no JPEGs with arithmetic coding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{173 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no 1-\/bit BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{174 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ GIF always returns *comp=4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{175 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{176 \textcolor{comment}{// Basic usage (see HDR discussion below for HDR usage):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{177 \textcolor{comment}{//    int x,y,n;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{178 \textcolor{comment}{//    unsigned char *data = stbi\_load(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{179 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... process data if not NULL ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{180 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... x = width, y = height, n = \# 8-\/bit components per pixel ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{181 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... replace '0' with '1'..'4' to force that many components per pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{182 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... but 'n' will always be the number that it would have been if you said 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{183 \textcolor{comment}{//    stbi\_image\_free(data)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{184 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{185 \textcolor{comment}{// Standard parameters:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{186 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *x                 -\/-\/ outputs image width in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{187 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *y                 -\/-\/ outputs image height in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{188 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *channels\_in\_file  -\/-\/ outputs \# of image components in image file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{189 \textcolor{comment}{//    int desired\_channels   -\/-\/ if non-\/zero, \# of image components requested in result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{190 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{191 \textcolor{comment}{// The return value from an image loader is an 'unsigned char *' which points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{192 \textcolor{comment}{// to the pixel data, or NULL on an allocation failure or if the image is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{193 \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt or invalid. The pixel data consists of *y scanlines of *x pixels,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{194 \textcolor{comment}{// with each pixel consisting of N interleaved 8-\/bit components; the first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{195 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel pointed to is top-\/left-\/most in the image. There is no padding between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{196 \textcolor{comment}{// image scanlines or between pixels, regardless of format. The number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{197 \textcolor{comment}{// components N is 'req\_comp' if req\_comp is non-\/zero, or *comp otherwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{198 \textcolor{comment}{// If req\_comp is non-\/zero, *comp has the number of components that \_would\_}}
\DoxyCodeLine{199 \textcolor{comment}{// have been output otherwise. E.g. if you set req\_comp to 4, you will always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{200 \textcolor{comment}{// get RGBA output, but you can check *comp to see if it's trivially opaque}}
\DoxyCodeLine{201 \textcolor{comment}{// because e.g. there were only 3 channels in the source image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{202 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{203 \textcolor{comment}{// An output image with N components has the following components interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{204 \textcolor{comment}{// in this order in each pixel:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{205 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{206 \textcolor{comment}{//     N=\#comp     components}}
\DoxyCodeLine{207 \textcolor{comment}{//       1           grey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{208 \textcolor{comment}{//       2           grey, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{209 \textcolor{comment}{//       3           red, green, blue}}
\DoxyCodeLine{210 \textcolor{comment}{//       4           red, green, blue, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{211 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{212 \textcolor{comment}{// If image loading fails for any reason, the return value will be NULL,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{213 \textcolor{comment}{// and *x, *y, *comp will be unchanged. The function stbi\_failure\_reason()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{214 \textcolor{comment}{// can be queried for an extremely brief, end-\/user unfriendly explanation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{215 \textcolor{comment}{// of why the load failed. Define STBI\_NO\_FAILURE\_STRINGS to avoid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{216 \textcolor{comment}{// compiling these strings at all, and STBI\_FAILURE\_USERMSG to get slightly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{217 \textcolor{comment}{// more user-\/friendly ones.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{218 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{219 \textcolor{comment}{// Paletted PNG, BMP, GIF, and PIC images are automatically depalettized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{220 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{221 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{222 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{223 \textcolor{comment}{// Philosophy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{224 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{225 \textcolor{comment}{// stb libraries are designed with the following priorities:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{226 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{227 \textcolor{comment}{//    1. easy to use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{228 \textcolor{comment}{//    2. easy to maintain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{229 \textcolor{comment}{//    3. good performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{230 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{231 \textcolor{comment}{// Sometimes I let "{}good performance"{} creep up in priority over "{}easy to maintain"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{232 \textcolor{comment}{// and for best performance I may provide less-\/easy-\/to-\/use APIs that give higher}}
\DoxyCodeLine{233 \textcolor{comment}{// performance, in addition to the easy to use ones. Nevertheless, it's important}}
\DoxyCodeLine{234 \textcolor{comment}{// to keep in mind that from the standpoint of you, a client of this library,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{235 \textcolor{comment}{// all you care about is \#1 and \#3, and stb libraries do not emphasize \#3 above all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{236 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{237 \textcolor{comment}{// Some secondary priorities arise directly from the first two, some of which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{238 \textcolor{comment}{// make more explicit reasons why performance can't be emphasized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{239 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{240 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Portable ("{}ease of use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{241 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Small footprint ("{}easy to maintain"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{242 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ No dependencies ("{}ease of use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{243 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{244 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{245 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{246 \textcolor{comment}{// I/O callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{247 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{248 \textcolor{comment}{// I/O callbacks allow you to read from arbitrary sources, like packaged}}
\DoxyCodeLine{249 \textcolor{comment}{// files or some other source. Data read from callbacks are processed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{250 \textcolor{comment}{// through a small internal buffer (currently 128 bytes) to try to reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{251 \textcolor{comment}{// overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{252 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{253 \textcolor{comment}{// The three functions you must define are "{}read"{} (reads some bytes of data),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{254 \textcolor{comment}{// "{}skip"{} (skips some bytes of data), "{}eof"{} (reports if the stream is at the end).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{255 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{256 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{257 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{258 \textcolor{comment}{// SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{259 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{260 \textcolor{comment}{// The JPEG decoder will try to automatically use SIMD kernels on x86 when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{261 \textcolor{comment}{// supported by the compiler. For ARM Neon support, you must explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{262 \textcolor{comment}{// request it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{263 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{264 \textcolor{comment}{// (The old do-\/it-\/yourself SIMD API is no longer supported in the current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{265 \textcolor{comment}{// code.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{266 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{267 \textcolor{comment}{// On x86, SSE2 will automatically be used when available based on a run-\/time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{268 \textcolor{comment}{// test; if not, the generic C versions are used as a fall-\/back. On ARM targets,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{269 \textcolor{comment}{// the typical path is to have separate builds for NEON and non-\/NEON devices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{270 \textcolor{comment}{// (at least this is true for iOS and Android). Therefore, the NEON support is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{271 \textcolor{comment}{// toggled by a build flag: define STBI\_NEON to get NEON loops.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{272 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{273 \textcolor{comment}{// The output of the JPEG decoder is slightly different from versions where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{274 \textcolor{comment}{// SIMD support was introduced (that is, for versions before 1.49). The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{275 \textcolor{comment}{// difference is only +-\/1 in the 8-\/bit RGB channels, and only on a small}}
\DoxyCodeLine{276 \textcolor{comment}{// fraction of pixels. You can force the pre-\/1.49 behavior by defining}}
\DoxyCodeLine{277 \textcolor{comment}{// STBI\_JPEG\_OLD, but this will disable some of the SIMD decoding path}}
\DoxyCodeLine{278 \textcolor{comment}{// and hence cost some performance.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{279 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{280 \textcolor{comment}{// If for some reason you do not want to use any of SIMD code, or if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{281 \textcolor{comment}{// you have issues compiling it, you can disable it entirely by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{282 \textcolor{comment}{// defining STBI\_NO\_SIMD.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{283 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{284 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{285 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{286 \textcolor{comment}{// HDR image support   (disable by defining STBI\_NO\_HDR)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{287 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{288 \textcolor{comment}{// stb\_image now supports loading HDR images in general, and currently}}
\DoxyCodeLine{289 \textcolor{comment}{// the Radiance .HDR file format, although the support is provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{290 \textcolor{comment}{// generically. You can still load any file through the existing interface;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{291 \textcolor{comment}{// if you attempt to load an HDR file, it will be automatically remapped to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{292 \textcolor{comment}{// LDR, assuming gamma 2.2 and an arbitrary scale factor defaulting to 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{293 \textcolor{comment}{// both of these constants can be reconfigured through this interface:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{294 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{295 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{296 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{297 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{298 \textcolor{comment}{// (note, do not use \_inverse\_ constants; stbi\_image will invert them}}
\DoxyCodeLine{299 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriately).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{300 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{301 \textcolor{comment}{// Additionally, there is a new, parallel interface for loading files as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{302 \textcolor{comment}{// (linear) floats to preserve the full dynamic range:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{303 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{304 \textcolor{comment}{//    float *data = stbi\_loadf(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{305 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{306 \textcolor{comment}{// If you load LDR images through this interface, those images will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{307 \textcolor{comment}{// be promoted to floating point values, run through the inverse of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{308 \textcolor{comment}{// constants corresponding to the above:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{309 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{310 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{311 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{312 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{313 \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, given a filename (or an open file or memory block-\/-\/see header}}
\DoxyCodeLine{314 \textcolor{comment}{// file for details) containing image data, you can query for the "{}most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{315 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriate"{} interface to use (that is, whether the image is HDR or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{316 \textcolor{comment}{// not), using:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{317 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{318 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_is\_hdr(char *filename);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{319 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{320 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{321 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{322 \textcolor{comment}{// iPhone PNG support:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{323 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{324 \textcolor{comment}{// By default we convert iphone-\/formatted PNGs back to RGB, even though}}
\DoxyCodeLine{325 \textcolor{comment}{// they are internally encoded differently. You can disable this conversion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{326 \textcolor{comment}{// by by calling stbi\_convert\_iphone\_png\_to\_rgb(0), in which case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{327 \textcolor{comment}{// you will always just get the native iphone "{}format"{} through (which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{328 \textcolor{comment}{// is BGR stored in RGB).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{329 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{330 \textcolor{comment}{// Call stbi\_set\_unpremultiply\_on\_load(1) as well to force a divide per}}
\DoxyCodeLine{331 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel to remove any premultiplied alpha *only* if the image file explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{332 \textcolor{comment}{// says there's premultiplied data (currently only happens in iPhone images,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{333 \textcolor{comment}{// and only if iPhone convert-\/to-\/rgb processing is on).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{334 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{335 }
\DoxyCodeLine{336 }

\DoxyCodeLine{628 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_\_MINGW32\_\_) \&\& defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET) \&\& !defined(STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2) \&\& !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{629 \textcolor{comment}{// Note that \_\_MINGW32\_\_ doesn't actually mean 32-\/bit, so we have to avoid STBI\_\_X64\_TARGET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{630 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{631 \textcolor{comment}{// 32-\/bit MinGW wants ESP to be 16-\/byte aligned, but this is not in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{632 \textcolor{comment}{// Windows ABI and VC++ as well as Windows DLLs don't maintain that invariant.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{633 \textcolor{comment}{// As a result, enabling SSE2 on 32-\/bit MinGW is dangerous when not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{634 \textcolor{comment}{// simultaneously enabling "{}-\/mstackrealign"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{635 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{636 \textcolor{comment}{// See https://github.com/nothings/stb/issues/81 for more information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{637 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{638 \textcolor{comment}{// So default to no SSE2 on 32-\/bit MinGW. If you've read this far and added}}
\DoxyCodeLine{639 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/mstackrealign to your build settings, feel free to \#define STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{640 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{641 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{878 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *stbi\_\_malloc(\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} size)}
\DoxyCodeLine{879 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{880     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} STBI\_MALLOC(size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{881 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{882 }
\DoxyCodeLine{883 \textcolor{comment}{// stb\_image uses ints pervasively, including for offset calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{884 \textcolor{comment}{// therefore the largest decoded image size we can support with the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{885 \textcolor{comment}{// current code, even on 64-\/bit targets, is INT\_MAX. this is not a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{886 \textcolor{comment}{// significant limitation for the intended use case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{887 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{888 \textcolor{comment}{// we do, however, need to make sure our size calculations don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{889 \textcolor{comment}{// overflow. hence a few helper functions for size calculations that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{890 \textcolor{comment}{// multiply integers together, making sure that they're non-\/negative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{891 \textcolor{comment}{// and no overflow occurs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{892 }
\DoxyCodeLine{893 \textcolor{comment}{// return 1 if the sum is valid, 0 on overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{894 \textcolor{comment}{// negative terms are considered invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{895 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_addsizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{896 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{897     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{898     \textcolor{comment}{// now 0 <= b <= INT\_MAX, hence also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{899     \textcolor{comment}{// 0 <= INT\_MAX -\/ b <= INTMAX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{900     \textcolor{comment}{// And "{}a + b <= INT\_MAX"{} (which might overflow) is the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{901     \textcolor{comment}{// same as a <= INT\_MAX -\/ b (no overflow)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{902     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a <= INT\_MAX -\/ b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{903 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{904 }
\DoxyCodeLine{905 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 1 if the product is valid, 0 on overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{906 \textcolor{comment}{// negative factors are considered invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{907 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{908 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{909     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (a < 0 || b < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{910     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b == 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1; \textcolor{comment}{// mul-\/by-\/0 is always safe}}
\DoxyCodeLine{911                           \textcolor{comment}{// portable way to check for no overflows in a*b}}
\DoxyCodeLine{912     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a <= INT\_MAX / b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{913 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{914 }
\DoxyCodeLine{915 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 1 if "{}a*b + add"{} has no negative terms/factors and doesn't overflow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{916 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_mad2sizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} add)}
\DoxyCodeLine{917 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{919 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{920 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1093                     image[(row * w + col) * channels + z] = image[((h -\/ row -\/ 1) * w + col) * channels + z];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1094                     image[((h -\/ row -\/ 1) * w + col) * channels + z] = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1095                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1096             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1097         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1098     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1640             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} z = data[i*comp + k] * 255 + 0.5f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1641             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z < 0) z = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1642             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z > 255) z = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1643             output[i*comp + k] = (stbi\_uc)stbi\_\_float2int(z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1644         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1645     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1646     STBI\_FREE(data);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1647     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} output;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1648 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1649 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1650 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1652 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1653 \textcolor{comment}{//  "{}baseline"{} JPEG/JFIF decoder}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1654 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1655 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1656 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't support delayed output of y-\/dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1657 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ simple interface (only one output format: 8-\/bit interleaved RGB)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1658 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't try to recover corrupt jpegs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1659 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't allow partial loading, loading multiple at once}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1660 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ still fast on x86 (copying globals into locals doesn't help x86)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1661 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ allocates lots of intermediate memory (full size of all components)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1662 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ non-\/interleaved case requires this anyway}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1663 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ allows good upsampling (see next)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1664 \textcolor{comment}{//    high-\/quality}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1665 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ upsampled channels are bilinearly interpolated, even across blocks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1666 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ quality integer IDCT derived from IJG's 'slow'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1667 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1668 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ fast huffman; reasonable integer IDCT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1669 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ some SIMD kernels for common paths on targets with SSE2/NEON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1670 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ uses a lot of intermediate memory, could cache poorly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1671 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1672 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1673 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1674 \textcolor{comment}{// huffman decoding acceleration}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1740 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_build\_huffman(stbi\_\_huffman *h, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *count)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1741 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1742     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j, k = 0, code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1743     \textcolor{comment}{// build size list for each symbol (from JPEG spec)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1744     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < 16; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1745         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < count[i]; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1746             h-\/>size[k++] = (stbi\_uc)(i + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1747     h-\/>size[k] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1748 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1749     \textcolor{comment}{// compute actual symbols (from jpeg spec)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1750     code = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1751     k = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1752     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 1; j <= 16; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1753         \textcolor{comment}{// compute delta to add to code to compute symbol id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1754         h-\/>delta[j] = k -\/ code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1755         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (h-\/>size[k] == j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1756             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (h-\/>size[k] == j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1757                 h-\/>code[k++] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(code++);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1758             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code -\/ 1 >= (1 << j)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad code lengths"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt JPEG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1759         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1760         \textcolor{comment}{// compute largest code + 1 for this size, preshifted as needed later}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1761         h-\/>maxcode[j] = code << (16 -\/ j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1762         code <<= 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1763     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1764     h-\/>maxcode[j] = 0xffffffff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1765 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1766     \textcolor{comment}{// build non-\/spec acceleration table; 255 is flag for not-\/accelerated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1767     memset(h-\/>fast, 255, 1 << FAST\_BITS);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1768     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < k; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1769         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} s = h-\/>size[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1770         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s <= FAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1771             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c = h-\/>code[i] << (FAST\_BITS -\/ s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1772             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} m = 1 << (FAST\_BITS -\/ s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1773             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < m; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1774                 h-\/>fast[c + j] = (stbi\_uc)i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1775             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1776         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1777     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1778     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1779 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1780 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1781 \textcolor{comment}{// build a table that decodes both magnitude and value of small ACs in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1782 \textcolor{comment}{// one go.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1783 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_build\_fast\_ac(stbi\_\_int16 *fast\_ac, stbi\_\_huffman *h)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1784 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1785     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1786     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < (1 << FAST\_BITS); ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1787         stbi\_uc fast = h-\/>fast[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1788         fast\_ac[i] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1789         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fast < 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1790             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rs = h-\/>values[fast];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1791             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} run = (rs >> 4) \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1792             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} magbits = rs \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1793             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} len = h-\/>size[fast];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1794 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1795             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (magbits \&\& len + magbits <= FAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1796                 \textcolor{comment}{// magnitude code followed by receive\_extend code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1797                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} k = ((i << len) \& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1)) >> (FAST\_BITS -\/ magbits);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1798                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} m = 1 << (magbits -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1799                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k < m) k += (-\/1 << magbits) + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1800                 \textcolor{comment}{// if the result is small enough, we can fit it in fast\_ac table}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1801                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k >= -\/128 \&\& k <= 127)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1802                     fast\_ac[i] = (stbi\_\_int16)((k << 8) + (run << 4) + (len + magbits));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1803             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1804         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1805     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1806 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1807 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1808 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(stbi\_\_jpeg *j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1809 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1810     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1811         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b = j-\/>nomore ? 0 : stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1812         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b == 0xff) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1813             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1814             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c != 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1815                 j-\/>marker = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1816                 j-\/>nomore = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1817                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1818             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1819         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1820         j-\/>code\_buffer |= b << (24 -\/ j-\/>code\_bits);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1821         j-\/>code\_bits += 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1822     \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (j-\/>code\_bits <= 24);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1823 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1824 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1825 \textcolor{comment}{// (1 << n) -\/ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1826 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_\_uint32 stbi\_\_bmask[17] = \{ 0,1,3,7,15,31,63,127,255,511,1023,2047,4095,8191,16383,32767,65535 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1827 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1828 \textcolor{comment}{// decode a jpeg huffman value from the bitstream}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1829 stbi\_inline \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_jpeg\_huff\_decode(stbi\_\_jpeg *j, stbi\_\_huffman *h)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1830 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1831     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1832     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c, k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1833 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1834     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>code\_bits < 16) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1835 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1836     \textcolor{comment}{// look at the top FAST\_BITS and determine what symbol ID it is,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1837     \textcolor{comment}{// if the code is <= FAST\_BITS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1838     c = (j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ FAST\_BITS)) \& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1839     k = h-\/>fast[c];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1840     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k < 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1841         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} s = h-\/>size[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1842         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s > j-\/>code\_bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1843             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1844         j-\/>code\_buffer <<= s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1845         j-\/>code\_bits -\/= s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1846         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} h-\/>values[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1847     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1848 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1849     \textcolor{comment}{// naive test is to shift the code\_buffer down so k bits are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1850     \textcolor{comment}{// valid, then test against maxcode. To speed this up, we've}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1851     \textcolor{comment}{// preshifted maxcode left so that it has (16-\/k) 0s at the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1852     \textcolor{comment}{// end; in other words, regardless of the number of bits, it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1853     \textcolor{comment}{// wants to be compared against something shifted to have 16;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1854     \textcolor{comment}{// that way we don't need to shift inside the loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1855     temp = j-\/>code\_buffer >> 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1856     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k = FAST\_BITS + 1; ; ++k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1857         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (temp < h-\/>maxcode[k])}
\DoxyCodeLine{1858             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1859     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k == 17) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1860         \textcolor{comment}{// error! code not found}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1861         j-\/>code\_bits -\/= 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1862         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1863     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1864 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1865     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k > j-\/>code\_bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1866         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1867 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1868     \textcolor{comment}{// convert the huffman code to the symbol id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1869     c = ((j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ k)) \& stbi\_\_bmask[k]) + h-\/>delta[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1870     STBI\_ASSERT((((j-\/>code\_buffer) >> (32 -\/ h-\/>size[c])) \& stbi\_\_bmask[h-\/>size[c]]) == h-\/>code[c]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1871 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1872     \textcolor{comment}{// convert the id to a symbol}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1873     j-\/>code\_bits -\/= k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1874     j-\/>code\_buffer <<= k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1875     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} h-\/>values[c];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1876 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1877 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1878 \textcolor{comment}{// bias[n] = (-\/1<<n) + 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1879 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_\_jbias[16] = \{ 0,-\/1,-\/3,-\/7,-\/15,-\/31,-\/63,-\/127,-\/255,-\/511,-\/1023,-\/2047,-\/4095,-\/8191,-\/16383,-\/32767 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{1881 \textcolor{comment}{// combined JPEG 'receive' and JPEG 'extend', since baseline}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1883 stbi\_inline \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_extend\_receive(stbi\_\_jpeg *j, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1884 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{1920 \textcolor{comment}{// given a value that's at position X in the zigzag stream,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2198 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_idct\_block(stbi\_uc *out, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_stride, \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} data[64])}

\DoxyCodeLine{2218                 \textcolor{comment}{// constants scaled things up by 1<<12; let's bring them back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2219                 \textcolor{comment}{// down, but keep 2 extra bits of precision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2220                 x0 += 512; x1 += 512; x2 += 512; x3 += 512;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2222             v[56] = (x0 -\/ t3) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2223             v[8] = (x1 + t2) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2224             v[48] = (x1 -\/ t2) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2225             v[16] = (x2 + t1) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2226             v[40] = (x2 -\/ t1) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2227             v[24] = (x3 + t0) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2228             v[32] = (x3 -\/ t0) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2229         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2230     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2231 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2232     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0, v = val, o = out; i < 8; ++i, v += 8, o += out\_stride) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2233         \textcolor{comment}{// no fast case since the first 1D IDCT spread components out}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2234         STBI\_\_IDCT\_1D(v[0], v[1], v[2], v[3], v[4], v[5], v[6], v[7])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2235             \textcolor{comment}{// constants scaled things up by 1<<12, plus we had 1<<2 from first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2236             \textcolor{comment}{// loop, plus horizontal and vertical each scale by sqrt(8) so together}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2237             \textcolor{comment}{// we've got an extra 1<<3, so 1<<17 total we need to remove.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2238             \textcolor{comment}{// so we want to round that, which means adding 0.5 * 1<<17,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2239             \textcolor{comment}{// aka 65536. Also, we'll end up with -\/128 to 127 that we want}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2240             \textcolor{comment}{// to encode as 0..255 by adding 128, so we'll add that before the shift}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2241             x0 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2242         x1 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2243         x2 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2244         x3 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2245         \textcolor{comment}{// tried computing the shifts into temps, or'ing the temps to see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2246         \textcolor{comment}{// if any were out of range, but that was slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2247         o[0] = stbi\_\_clamp((x0 + t3) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2248         o[7] = stbi\_\_clamp((x0 -\/ t3) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2249         o[1] = stbi\_\_clamp((x1 + t2) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2250         o[6] = stbi\_\_clamp((x1 -\/ t2) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2251         o[2] = stbi\_\_clamp((x2 + t1) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2252         o[5] = stbi\_\_clamp((x2 -\/ t1) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2253         o[3] = stbi\_\_clamp((x3 + t0) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2254         o[4] = stbi\_\_clamp((x3 -\/ t0) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2255     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2256 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2257 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2258 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_SSE2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2259 \textcolor{comment}{// sse2 integer IDCT. not the fastest possible implementation but it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2260 \textcolor{comment}{// produces bit-\/identical results to the generic C version so it's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2261 \textcolor{comment}{// fully "{}transparent"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2262 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_idct\_simd(stbi\_uc *out, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_stride, \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} data[64])}

\DoxyCodeLine{2268     \textcolor{comment}{// dot product constant: even elems=x, odd elems=y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2269 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define dct\_const(x,y)  \_mm\_setr\_epi16((x),(y),(x),(y),(x),(y),(x),(y))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2270 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2271     \textcolor{comment}{// out(0) = c0[even]*x + c0[odd]*y   (c0, x, y 16-\/bit, out 32-\/bit)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2272     \textcolor{comment}{// out(1) = c1[even]*x + c1[odd]*y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2273 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define dct\_rot(out0,out1, x,y,c0,c1) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2274 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i c0\#\#lo = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16((x),(y)); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2275 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i c0\#\#hi = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16((x),(y)); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2276 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out0\#\#\_l = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#lo, c0); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2277 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out0\#\#\_h = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#hi, c0); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2278 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out1\#\#\_l = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#lo, c1); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2279 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out1\#\#\_h = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#hi, c1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2280 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2281     \textcolor{comment}{// out = in << 12  (in 16-\/bit, out 32-\/bit)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2282 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define dct\_widen(out, in) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2283 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out\#\#\_l = \_mm\_srai\_epi32(\_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), (in)), 4); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2284 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out\#\#\_h = \_mm\_srai\_epi32(\_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), (in)), 4)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2285 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2286     \textcolor{comment}{// wide add}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2647 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_MARKER\_none  0xff}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2648 \textcolor{comment}{// if there's a pending marker from the entropy stream, return that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2649 \textcolor{comment}{// otherwise, fetch from the stream and get a marker. if there's no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2650 \textcolor{comment}{// marker, return 0xff, which is never a valid marker value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2651 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc stbi\_\_get\_marker(stbi\_\_jpeg *j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2652 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2653     stbi\_uc x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2654     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>marker != STBI\_\_MARKER\_none) \{ x = j-\/>marker; j-\/>marker = STBI\_\_MARKER\_none; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} x; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2655     x = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2656     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x != 0xff) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} STBI\_\_MARKER\_none;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2657     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (x == 0xff)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2658         x = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2659     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2660 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2661 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2662 \textcolor{comment}{// in each scan, we'll have scan\_n components, and the order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2663 \textcolor{comment}{// of the components is specified by order[]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2664 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_RESTART(x)     ((x) >= 0xd0 \&\& (x) <= 0xd7)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2665 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2666 \textcolor{comment}{// after a restart interval, stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset the entropy decoder and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2667 \textcolor{comment}{// the dc prediction}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2668 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset(stbi\_\_jpeg *j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2669 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2670     j-\/>code\_bits = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2671     j-\/>code\_buffer = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2672     j-\/>nomore = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2673     j-\/>img\_comp[0].dc\_pred = j-\/>img\_comp[1].dc\_pred = j-\/>img\_comp[2].dc\_pred = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2674     j-\/>marker = STBI\_\_MARKER\_none;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2675     j-\/>todo = j-\/>restart\_interval ? j-\/>restart\_interval : 0x7fffffff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2676     j-\/>eob\_run = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2677     \textcolor{comment}{// no more than 1<<31 MCUs if no restart\_interal? that's plenty safe,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2678     \textcolor{comment}{// since we don't even allow 1<<30 pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2679 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2680 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2681 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_parse\_entropy\_coded\_data(stbi\_\_jpeg *z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2682 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2683     stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset(z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2684     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!z-\/>progressive) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2685         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>scan\_n == 1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2686             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2687             STBI\_SIMD\_ALIGN(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}, data[64]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2688             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n = z-\/>order[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2689             \textcolor{comment}{// non-\/interleaved data, we just need to process one block at a time,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2690             \textcolor{comment}{// in trivial scanline order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2691             \textcolor{comment}{// number of blocks to do just depends on how many actual "{}pixels"{} this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2692             \textcolor{comment}{// component has, independent of interleaved MCU blocking and such}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2693             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w = (z-\/>img\_comp[n].x + 7) >> 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2694             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} h = (z-\/>img\_comp[n].y + 7) >> 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2695             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < h; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2696                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2697                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} ha = z-\/>img\_comp[n].ha;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2698                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_jpeg\_decode\_block(z, data, z-\/>huff\_dc + z-\/>img\_comp[n].hd, z-\/>huff\_ac + ha, z-\/>fast\_ac[ha], n, z-\/>dequant[z-\/>img\_comp[n].tq])) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2699                     z-\/>idct\_block\_kernel(z-\/>img\_comp[n].data + z-\/>img\_comp[n].w2*j * 8 + i * 8, z-\/>img\_comp[n].w2, data);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2700                     \textcolor{comment}{// every data block is an MCU, so countdown the restart interval}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2701                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (-\/-\/z-\/>todo <= 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2702                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>code\_bits < 24) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2703                         \textcolor{comment}{// if it's NOT a restart, then just bail, so we get corrupt data}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3213     \textcolor{comment}{// process groups of 8 pixels for as long as we can.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3214     \textcolor{comment}{// note we can't handle the last pixel in a row in this loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3215     \textcolor{comment}{// because we need to handle the filter boundary conditions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3216     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i < ((w -\/ 1) \& \string~7); i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3217 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(STBI\_SSE2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3218         \textcolor{comment}{// load and perform the vertical filtering pass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3219         \textcolor{comment}{// this uses 3*x + y = 4*x + (y -\/ x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3220         \_\_m128i zero = \_mm\_setzero\_si128();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3221         \_\_m128i farb = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) (in\_far + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3222         \_\_m128i nearb = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) (in\_near + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3223         \_\_m128i farw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(farb, zero);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3224         \_\_m128i nearw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(nearb, zero);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3225         \_\_m128i diff = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(farw, nearw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3226         \_\_m128i nears = \_mm\_slli\_epi16(nearw, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3227         \_\_m128i curr = \_mm\_add\_epi16(nears, diff); \textcolor{comment}{// current row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3228 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3229                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter works the same based on shifted vers of current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3230                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// row. "{}prev"{} is current row shifted right by 1 pixel; we need to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3231                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// insert the previous pixel value (from t1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3232                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// "{}next"{} is current row shifted left by 1 pixel, with first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3233                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// of next block of 8 pixels added in.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3234         \_\_m128i prv0 = \_mm\_slli\_si128(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3235         \_\_m128i nxt0 = \_mm\_srli\_si128(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3236         \_\_m128i prev = \_mm\_insert\_epi16(prv0, t1, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3237         \_\_m128i next = \_mm\_insert\_epi16(nxt0, 3 * in\_near[i + 8] + in\_far[i + 8], 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3238 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3239         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter, polyphase implementation since it's convenient:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3240         \textcolor{comment}{// even pixels = 3*cur + prev = cur*4 + (prev -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3241         \textcolor{comment}{// odd  pixels = 3*cur + next = cur*4 + (next -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3242         \textcolor{comment}{// note the shared term.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3243         \_\_m128i bias = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3244         \_\_m128i curs = \_mm\_slli\_epi16(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3245         \_\_m128i prvd = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(prev, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3246         \_\_m128i nxtd = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(next, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3247         \_\_m128i curb = \_mm\_add\_epi16(curs, bias);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3248         \_\_m128i even = \_mm\_add\_epi16(prvd, curb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3249         \_\_m128i odd = \_mm\_add\_epi16(nxtd, curb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3250 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3251         \textcolor{comment}{// interleave even and odd pixels, then undo scaling.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3252         \_\_m128i int0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(even, odd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3253         \_\_m128i int1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(even, odd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3254         \_\_m128i de0 = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(int0, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3255         \_\_m128i de1 = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(int1, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3256 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3257         \textcolor{comment}{// pack and write output}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3258         \_\_m128i outv = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(de0, de1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3259         \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i *) (out + i * 2), outv);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3260 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif defined(STBI\_NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3261         \textcolor{comment}{// load and perform the vertical filtering pass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3262         \textcolor{comment}{// this uses 3*x + y = 4*x + (y -\/ x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3263         uint8x8\_t farb = vld1\_u8(in\_far + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3264         uint8x8\_t nearb = vld1\_u8(in\_near + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3265         int16x8\_t diff = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vsubl\_u8(farb, nearb));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3266         int16x8\_t nears = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vshll\_n\_u8(nearb, 2));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3267         int16x8\_t curr = vaddq\_s16(nears, diff); \textcolor{comment}{// current row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3268 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3269                                                  \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter works the same based on shifted vers of current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3270                                                  \textcolor{comment}{// row. "{}prev"{} is current row shifted right by 1 pixel; we need to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3271                                                  \textcolor{comment}{// insert the previous pixel value (from t1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3272                                                  \textcolor{comment}{// "{}next"{} is current row shifted left by 1 pixel, with first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3273                                                  \textcolor{comment}{// of next block of 8 pixels added in.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3274         int16x8\_t prv0 = vextq\_s16(curr, curr, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3275         int16x8\_t nxt0 = vextq\_s16(curr, curr, 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3276         int16x8\_t prev = vsetq\_lane\_s16(t1, prv0, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3277         int16x8\_t next = vsetq\_lane\_s16(3 * in\_near[i + 8] + in\_far[i + 8], nxt0, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3278 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3279         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter, polyphase implementation since it's convenient:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3280         \textcolor{comment}{// even pixels = 3*cur + prev = cur*4 + (prev -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3281         \textcolor{comment}{// odd  pixels = 3*cur + next = cur*4 + (next -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3282         \textcolor{comment}{// note the shared term.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3283         int16x8\_t curs = vshlq\_n\_s16(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3284         int16x8\_t prvd = vsubq\_s16(prev, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3285         int16x8\_t nxtd = vsubq\_s16(next, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3286         int16x8\_t even = vaddq\_s16(curs, prvd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3287         int16x8\_t odd = vaddq\_s16(curs, nxtd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3288 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3289         \textcolor{comment}{// undo scaling and round, then store with even/odd phases interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3290         uint8x8x2\_t o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3291         o.val[0] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(even, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3292         o.val[1] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(odd, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3293         vst2\_u8(out + i * 2, o);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3294 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3295 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3296         \textcolor{comment}{// "{}previous"{} value for next iter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3297         t1 = 3 * in\_near[i + 7] + in\_far[i + 7];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3298     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3299 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3300     t0 = t1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3301     t1 = 3 * in\_near[i] + in\_far[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3302     out[i * 2] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t1 + t0 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3303 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3304     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (++i; i < w; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3305         t0 = t1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3306         t1 = 3 * in\_near[i] + in\_far[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3307         out[i * 2 -\/ 1] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t0 + t1 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3308         out[i * 2] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t1 + t0 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3309     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3310     out[w * 2 -\/ 1] = stbi\_\_div4(t1 + 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3311 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3312     STBI\_NOTUSED(hs);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3313 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3314     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3315 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3316 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3317 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3318 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc *stbi\_\_resample\_row\_generic(stbi\_uc *out, stbi\_uc *in\_near, stbi\_uc *in\_far, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} hs)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3319 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3320     \textcolor{comment}{// resample with nearest-\/neighbor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3321     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3322     STBI\_NOTUSED(in\_far);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3323     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3324         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < hs; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3325             out[i*hs + j] = in\_near[i];}

\DoxyCodeLine{3327 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3329 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_JPEG\_OLD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3330 \textcolor{comment}{// this is the same YCbCr-\/to-\/RGB calculation that stb\_image has used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3331 \textcolor{comment}{// historically before the algorithm changes in 1.49}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3332 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define float2fixed(x)  ((int) ((x) * 65536 + 0.5))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3333 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_YCbCr\_to\_RGB\_row(stbi\_uc *out, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc *y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc *pcb, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc *pcr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} step)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3334 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3335     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3336     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < count; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3337         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y\_fixed = (y[i] << 16) + 32768; \textcolor{comment}{// rounding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3338         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r, g, b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3339         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cr = pcr[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3340         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cb = pcb[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3341         r = y\_fixed + cr*float2fixed(1.40200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3342         g = y\_fixed -\/ cr*float2fixed(0.71414f) -\/ cb*float2fixed(0.34414f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3343         b = y\_fixed + cb*float2fixed(1.77200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3344         r >>= 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3345         g >>= 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3346         b >>= 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3347         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})r > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r < 0) r = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} r = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3348         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})g > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g < 0) g = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} g = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3349         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})b > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) b = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} b = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3350         out[0] = (stbi\_uc)r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3351         out[1] = (stbi\_uc)g;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3352         out[2] = (stbi\_uc)b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3353         out[3] = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3354         out += step;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3355     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3356 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3357 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3358 \textcolor{comment}{// this is a reduced-\/precision calculation of YCbCr-\/to-\/RGB introduced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3359 \textcolor{comment}{// to make sure the code produces the same results in both SIMD and scalar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3360 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define float2fixed(x)  (((int) ((x) * 4096.0f + 0.5f)) << 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3361 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_YCbCr\_to\_RGB\_row(stbi\_uc *out, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc *y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc *pcb, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc *pcr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} step)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3362 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3363     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3364     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < count; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3365         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y\_fixed = (y[i] << 20) + (1 << 19); \textcolor{comment}{// rounding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3366         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r, g, b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3367         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cr = pcr[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3368         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cb = pcb[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3369         r = y\_fixed + cr* float2fixed(1.40200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3370         g = y\_fixed + (cr*-\/float2fixed(0.71414f)) + ((cb*-\/float2fixed(0.34414f)) \& 0xffff0000);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3371         b = y\_fixed + cb* float2fixed(1.77200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3372         r >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3373         g >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3374         b >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3375         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})r > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r < 0) r = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} r = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3376         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})g > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g < 0) g = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} g = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3377         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})b > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) b = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} b = 255; \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3379         out[1] = (stbi\_uc)g;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3380         out[2] = (stbi\_uc)b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3381         out[3] = 255;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3386 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3387 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(STBI\_SSE2) || defined(STBI\_NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3388 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_YCbCr\_to\_RGB\_simd(stbi\_uc *out, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const} *y, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const} *pcb, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const} *pcr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} step)}

\DoxyCodeLine{3392 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_SSE2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3393     \textcolor{comment}{// step == 3 is pretty ugly on the final interleave, and i'm not convinced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3394     \textcolor{comment}{// it's useful in practice (you wouldn't use it for textures, for example).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3395     \textcolor{comment}{// so just accelerate step == 4 case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3396     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (step == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3397         \textcolor{comment}{// this is a fairly straightforward implementation and not super-\/optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3398         \_\_m128i signflip = \_mm\_set1\_epi8(-\/0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3399         \_\_m128i cr\_const0 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.40200f*4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3400         \_\_m128i cr\_const1 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.71414f*4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3401         \_\_m128i cb\_const0 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.34414f*4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3402         \_\_m128i cb\_const1 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.77200f*4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3403         \_\_m128i y\_bias = \_mm\_set1\_epi8((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char})(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char})128);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3404         \_\_m128i xw = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(255); \textcolor{comment}{// alpha channel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3405 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3406         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i + 7 < count; i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3407             \textcolor{comment}{// load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3408             \_\_m128i y\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) (y + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3409             \_\_m128i cr\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) (pcr + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3410             \_\_m128i cb\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i *) (pcb + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3411             \_\_m128i cr\_biased = \_mm\_xor\_si128(cr\_bytes, signflip); \textcolor{comment}{// -\/128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3412             \_\_m128i cb\_biased = \_mm\_xor\_si128(cb\_bytes, signflip); \textcolor{comment}{// -\/128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3413 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3414                                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// unpack to short (and left-\/shift cr, cb by 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3415             \_\_m128i yw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(y\_bias, y\_bytes);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3416             \_\_m128i crw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), cr\_biased);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3417             \_\_m128i cbw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), cb\_biased);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3418 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3419             \textcolor{comment}{// color transform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3420             \_\_m128i yws = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(yw, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3421             \_\_m128i cr0 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cr\_const0, crw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3422             \_\_m128i cb0 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cb\_const0, cbw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3423             \_\_m128i cb1 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cbw, cb\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3424             \_\_m128i cr1 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(crw, cr\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3425             \_\_m128i rws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(cr0, yws);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3426             \_\_m128i gwt = \_mm\_add\_epi16(cb0, yws);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3427             \_\_m128i bws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(yws, cb1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3428             \_\_m128i gws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(gwt, cr1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3429 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3430             \textcolor{comment}{// descale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3431             \_\_m128i rw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(rws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3432             \_\_m128i bw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(bws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3433             \_\_m128i gw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(gws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3434 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3435             \textcolor{comment}{// back to byte, set up for transpose}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3436             \_\_m128i brb = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(rw, bw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3437             \_\_m128i gxb = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(gw, xw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3438 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3439             \textcolor{comment}{// transpose to interleave channels}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3441             \_\_m128i t1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi8(brb, gxb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3442             \_\_m128i o0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(t0, t1);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3447             \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i *) (out + 16), o1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3448             out += 32;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3449         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3450     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3451 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3452 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3453 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_NEON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3454     \textcolor{comment}{// in this version, step=3 support would be easy to add. but is there demand?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3455     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (step == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3456         \textcolor{comment}{// this is a fairly straightforward implementation and not super-\/optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3457         uint8x8\_t signflip = vdup\_n\_u8(0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3458         int16x8\_t cr\_const0 = vdupq\_n\_s16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.40200f*4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3459         int16x8\_t cr\_const1 = vdupq\_n\_s16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.71414f*4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3460         int16x8\_t cb\_const0 = vdupq\_n\_s16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.34414f*4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3461         int16x8\_t cb\_const1 = vdupq\_n\_s16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.77200f*4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3462 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3463         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i + 7 < count; i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3464             \textcolor{comment}{// load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3465             uint8x8\_t y\_bytes = vld1\_u8(y + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3466             uint8x8\_t cr\_bytes = vld1\_u8(pcr + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3467             uint8x8\_t cb\_bytes = vld1\_u8(pcb + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3468             int8x8\_t cr\_biased = vreinterpret\_s8\_u8(vsub\_u8(cr\_bytes, signflip));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3469             int8x8\_t cb\_biased = vreinterpret\_s8\_u8(vsub\_u8(cb\_bytes, signflip));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3470 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3471             \textcolor{comment}{// expand to s16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3472             int16x8\_t yws = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vshll\_n\_u8(y\_bytes, 4));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3473             int16x8\_t crw = vshll\_n\_s8(cr\_biased, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3474             int16x8\_t cbw = vshll\_n\_s8(cb\_biased, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3475 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3476             \textcolor{comment}{// color transform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3477             int16x8\_t cr0 = vqdmulhq\_s16(crw, cr\_const0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3478             int16x8\_t cb0 = vqdmulhq\_s16(cbw, cb\_const0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3479             int16x8\_t cr1 = vqdmulhq\_s16(crw, cr\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3480             int16x8\_t cb1 = vqdmulhq\_s16(cbw, cb\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3481             int16x8\_t rws = vaddq\_s16(yws, cr0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3482             int16x8\_t gws = vaddq\_s16(vaddq\_s16(yws, cb0), cr1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3483             int16x8\_t bws = vaddq\_s16(yws, cb1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3484 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3485             \textcolor{comment}{// undo scaling, round, convert to byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3486             uint8x8x4\_t o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3487             o.val[0] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(rws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3488             o.val[1] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(gws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3489             o.val[2] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(bws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3490             o.val[3] = vdup\_n\_u8(255);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3491 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3492             \textcolor{comment}{// store, interleaving r/g/b/a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3493             vst4\_u8(out, o);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3494             out += 8 * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3495         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3496     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3497 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3498 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3499     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i < count; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3500         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y\_fixed = (y[i] << 20) + (1 << 19); \textcolor{comment}{// rounding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r, g, b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3502         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cr = pcr[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3503         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cb = pcb[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504         r = y\_fixed + cr* float2fixed(1.40200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3505         g = y\_fixed + cr*-\/float2fixed(0.71414f) + ((cb*-\/float2fixed(0.34414f)) \& 0xffff0000);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3506         b = y\_fixed + cb* float2fixed(1.77200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3507         r >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3508         g >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3509         b >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3510         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})r > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r < 0) r = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} r = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3511         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})g > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g < 0) g = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} g = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3512         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})b > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) b = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} b = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3513         out[0] = (stbi\_uc)r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3514         out[1] = (stbi\_uc)g;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3515         out[2] = (stbi\_uc)b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3516         out[3] = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3517         out += step;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3518     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3519 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3520 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3719 \textcolor{comment}{// public domain zlib decode    v0.2  Sean Barrett 2006-\/11-\/18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3720 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3721 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all input must be provided in an upfront buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3722 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all output is written to a single output buffer (can malloc/realloc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3723 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3724 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ fast huffman}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3725 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3726 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_ZLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3727 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3728 \textcolor{comment}{// fast-\/way is faster to check than jpeg huffman, but slow way is slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3729 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS  9 }\textcolor{comment}{// accelerate all cases in default tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3730 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZFAST\_MASK  ((1 << STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS) -\/ 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3731 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3732 \textcolor{comment}{// zlib-\/style huffman encoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3733 \textcolor{comment}{// (jpegs packs from left, zlib from right, so can't share code)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3734 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3735 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3736     stbi\_\_uint16 fast[1 << STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3737     stbi\_\_uint16 firstcode[16];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3738     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} maxcode[17];}

\DoxyCodeLine{3744 stbi\_inline \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_bitreverse16(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3745 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3746     n = ((n \& 0xAAAA) >> 1) | ((n \& 0x5555) << 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3747     n = ((n \& 0xCCCC) >> 2) | ((n \& 0x3333) << 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3748     n = ((n \& 0xF0F0) >> 4) | ((n \& 0x0F0F) << 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3749     n = ((n \& 0xFF00) >> 8) | ((n \& 0x00FF) << 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3750     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3751 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3752 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3753 stbi\_inline \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_bit\_reverse(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} v, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3754 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3755     STBI\_ASSERT(bits <= 16);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3756     \textcolor{comment}{// to bit reverse n bits, reverse 16 and shift}}
