\DoxyCodeLine{3758     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_bitreverse16(v) >> (16 -\/ bits);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3761 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_zbuild\_huffman(stbi\_\_zhuffman *z, stbi\_uc *sizelist, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} num)}

\DoxyCodeLine{3763     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, k = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3764     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} code, next\_code[16], sizes[17];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3765 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3766     \textcolor{comment}{// DEFLATE spec for generating codes}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3768     memset(z-\/>fast, 0, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(z-\/>fast));}

\DoxyCodeLine{3779         z-\/>firstsymbol[i] = (stbi\_\_uint16)k;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3784         code <<= 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3785         k += sizes[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3786     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3787     z-\/>maxcode[16] = 0x10000; \textcolor{comment}{// sentinel}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3799                     j += (1 << s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3800                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3801             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3802             ++next\_code[s];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3803         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3804     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4188 \textcolor{comment}{// public domain "{}baseline"{} PNG decoder   v0.10  Sean Barrett 2006-\/11-\/18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4189 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4190 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ only 8-\/bit samples}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4191 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ no CRC checking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4192 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ allocates lots of intermediate memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4193 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ avoids problem of streaming data between subsystems}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4194 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ avoids explicit window management}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4195 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4196 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ uses stb\_zlib, a PD zlib implementation with fast huffman decoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4197 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4309         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k = 0; k < filter\_bytes; ++k) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4311             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_none: cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4312             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_sub: cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4313             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_up: cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + prior[k]); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4314             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_avg: cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + (prior[k] >> 1)); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}

\DoxyCodeLine{4316             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_avg\_first: cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4317             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_paeth\_first: cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4318             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4319         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4320 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4321         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 8) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4326             prior += out\_n;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4334             cur += output\_bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4335             prior += output\_bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4336         \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4340             prior += 1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4482 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_create\_png\_image(stbi\_\_png *a, stbi\_uc *image\_data, stbi\_\_uint32 image\_data\_len, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_n, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} depth, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} color, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} interlaced)}

\DoxyCodeLine{4495         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} yorig[] = \{ 0,0,4,0,2,0,1 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4496         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} xspc[] = \{ 8,8,4,4,2,2,1 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4497         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} yspc[] = \{ 8,8,8,4,4,2,2 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{4499         \textcolor{comment}{// pass1\_x[4] = 0, pass1\_x[5] = 1, pass1\_x[12] = 1}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4526 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_compute\_transparency(stbi\_\_png *z, stbi\_uc tc[3], \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_n)}

\DoxyCodeLine{5357 \textcolor{comment}{// read 16bit value and convert to 24bit RGB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5358 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_tga\_read\_rgb16(stbi\_\_context *s, stbi\_uc* out)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5359 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5360     stbi\_\_uint16 px = (stbi\_\_uint16)stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5361     stbi\_\_uint16 fiveBitMask = 31;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5362     \textcolor{comment}{// we have 3 channels with 5bits each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5363     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r = (px >> 10) \& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5364     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} g = (px >> 5) \& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5365     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b = px \& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5366     \textcolor{comment}{// Note that this saves the data in RGB(A) order, so it doesn't need to be swapped later}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5367     out[0] = (stbi\_uc)((r * 255) / 31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5368     out[1] = (stbi\_uc)((g * 255) / 31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5369     out[2] = (stbi\_uc)((b * 255) / 31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5370 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5371     \textcolor{comment}{// some people claim that the most significant bit might be used for alpha}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5589 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_psd\_decode\_rle(stbi\_\_context *s, stbi\_uc *p, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pixelCount)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5590 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5591     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, nleft, len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5592 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5593     count = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5594     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((nleft = pixelCount -\/ count) > 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5595         len = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5596         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len == 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5597             \textcolor{comment}{// No-\/op.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5598         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5599         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len < 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5600             \textcolor{comment}{// Copy next len+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5601             len++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5602             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > nleft) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5603             count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5604             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5605                 *p = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5606                 p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5607                 len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5608             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5609         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5610         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5611             stbi\_uc   val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5612             \textcolor{comment}{// Next -\/len+1 bytes in the dest are replicated from next source byte.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5613             \textcolor{comment}{// (Interpret len as a negative 8-\/bit int.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5614             len = 257 -\/ len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5615             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > nleft) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5616             val = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5617             count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5618             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5619                 *p = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5620                 p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5621                 len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5622             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5623         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5624     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5625 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5626     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5627 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5657     w = stbi\_\_get32be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5658 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5659     \textcolor{comment}{// Make sure the depth is 8 bits.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5660     bitdepth = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5661     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth != 8 \&\& bitdepth != 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5662         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}unsupported bit depth"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD bit depth is not 8 or 16 bit"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5663 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5664     \textcolor{comment}{// Make sure the color mode is RGB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5665     \textcolor{comment}{// Valid options are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5666     \textcolor{comment}{//   0: Bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5667     \textcolor{comment}{//   1: Grayscale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5668     \textcolor{comment}{//   2: Indexed color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5669     \textcolor{comment}{//   3: RGB color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5670     \textcolor{comment}{//   4: CMYK color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5671     \textcolor{comment}{//   7: Multichannel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5672     \textcolor{comment}{//   8: Duotone}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5673     \textcolor{comment}{//   9: Lab color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5674     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get16be(s) != 3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5675         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong color format"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD is not in RGB color format"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5676 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5677     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the Mode Data.  (It's the palette for indexed color; other info for other modes.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5678     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{5679 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5680     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the image resources.  (resolution, pen tool paths, etc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5681     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{5682 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5683     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the reserved data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5684     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{5685 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5686     \textcolor{comment}{// Find out if the data is compressed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5687     \textcolor{comment}{// Known values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5688     \textcolor{comment}{//   0: no compression}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5689     \textcolor{comment}{//   1: RLE compressed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5690     compression = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5691     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (compression > 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5692         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad compression"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD has an unknown compression format"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5693 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5694     \textcolor{comment}{// Check size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5695     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_mad3sizes\_valid(4, w, h, 0))}
\DoxyCodeLine{5696         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PSD"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5697 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5698     \textcolor{comment}{// Create the destination image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5699 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5700     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!compression \&\& bitdepth == 16 \&\& bpc == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5701         out = (stbi\_uc *)stbi\_\_malloc\_mad3(8, w, h, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5702         ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel = 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5703     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5704     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5705         out = (stbi\_uc *)stbi\_\_malloc(4 * w*h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5706 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5707     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!out) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}outofmem"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Out of memory"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5708     pixelCount = w*h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5709 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5710     \textcolor{comment}{// Initialize the data to zero.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5711     \textcolor{comment}{//memset( out, 0, pixelCount * 4 );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5712 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5713     \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, the image data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5714     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (compression) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5715         \textcolor{comment}{// RLE as used by .PSD and .TIFF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5716         \textcolor{comment}{// Loop until you get the number of unpacked bytes you are expecting:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5717         \textcolor{comment}{//     Read the next source byte into n.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5718         \textcolor{comment}{//     If n is between 0 and 127 inclusive, copy the next n+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5719         \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is between -\/127 and -\/1 inclusive, copy the next byte -\/n+1 times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5720         \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is 128, noop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5721         \textcolor{comment}{// Endloop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5722 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5723         \textcolor{comment}{// The RLE-\/compressed data is preceeded by a 2-\/byte data count for each row in the data,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5724         \textcolor{comment}{// which we're going to just skip.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5725         stbi\_\_skip(s, h * channelCount * 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5726 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5727         \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5728         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5729             stbi\_uc *p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5730 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5731             p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5732             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel >= channelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5733                 \textcolor{comment}{// Fill this channel with default data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5734                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5735                     *p = (channel == 3 ? 255 : 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5736             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5737             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5738                 \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5739                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_psd\_decode\_rle(s, p, pixelCount)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5740                     STBI\_FREE(out);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5741                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}corrupt"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad RLE data"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5742                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5743             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5744         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5745 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5746     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5747     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5748         \textcolor{comment}{// We're at the raw image data.  It's each channel in order (Red, Green, Blue, Alpha, ...)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5749         \textcolor{comment}{// where each channel consists of an 8-\/bit (or 16-\/bit) value for each pixel in the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5750 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5751         \textcolor{comment}{// Read the data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5752         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5753             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel >= channelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5754                 \textcolor{comment}{// Fill this channel with default data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5755                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth == 16 \&\& bpc == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5756                     stbi\_\_uint16 *q = ((stbi\_\_uint16 *)out) + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5757                     stbi\_\_uint16 val = channel == 3 ? 65535 : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5758                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, q += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5759                         *q = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5760                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5761                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5762                     stbi\_uc *p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5763                     stbi\_uc val = channel == 3 ? 255 : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5764                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5765                         *p = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5766                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5767             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5768             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5769                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16) \{    \textcolor{comment}{// output bpc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5770                     stbi\_\_uint16 *q = ((stbi\_\_uint16 *)out) + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5771                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, q += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5772                         *q = (stbi\_\_uint16)stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5773                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5774                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5775                     stbi\_uc *p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5776                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth == 16) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// input bpc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5777                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5778                             *p = (stbi\_uc)(stbi\_\_get16be(s) >> 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5779                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5780                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5781                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5782                             *p = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5783                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5784                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5785             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5786         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5787     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5788 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5789     \textcolor{comment}{// remove weird white matte from PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5790     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channelCount >= 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5791         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5792             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w*h; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5793                 stbi\_\_uint16 *pixel = (stbi\_\_uint16 *)out + 4 * i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5794                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pixel[3] != 0 \&\& pixel[3] != 65535) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5795                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = pixel[3] / 65535.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5796                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ra = 1.0f / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5797                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inv\_a = 65535.0f * (1 -\/ ra);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5798                     pixel[0] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[0] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5799                     pixel[1] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[1] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5800                     pixel[2] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[2] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5801                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5802             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5803         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5804         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5805             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w*h; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5806                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *pixel = out + 4 * i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5807                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pixel[3] != 0 \&\& pixel[3] != 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5808                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = pixel[3] / 255.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5809                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ra = 1.0f / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5810                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inv\_a = 255.0f * (1 -\/ ra);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5811                     pixel[0] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[0] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5812                     pixel[1] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[1] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5813                     pixel[2] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[2] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5814                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5815             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5816         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5817     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5818 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5819     \textcolor{comment}{// convert to desired output format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5820     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp \&\& req\_comp != 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5821         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5822             out = (stbi\_uc *)stbi\_\_convert\_format16((stbi\_\_uint16 *)out, 4, req\_comp, w, h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5823         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5824             out = stbi\_\_convert\_format(out, 4, req\_comp, w, h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5825         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (out == NULL) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out; \textcolor{comment}{// stbi\_\_convert\_format frees input on failure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5826     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5827 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5828     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (comp) *comp = 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5829     *y = h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5830     *x = w;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5831 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5832     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5833 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5834 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5835 }

\DoxyCodeLine{5898 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc *stbi\_\_pic\_load\_core(stbi\_\_context *s, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} width, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} height, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *comp, stbi\_uc *result)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5899 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5900     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} act\_comp = 0, num\_packets = 0, y, chained;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5901     stbi\_\_pic\_packet packets[10];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5902 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5903     \textcolor{comment}{// this will (should...) cater for even some bizarre stuff like having data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5904     \textcolor{comment}{// for the same channel in multiple packets.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5905     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5906         stbi\_\_pic\_packet *packet;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5907 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5908         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (num\_packets == \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(packets) / \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(packets[0]))}

\DoxyCodeLine{5924     *comp = (act\_comp \& 0x10 ? 4 : 3); \textcolor{comment}{// has alpha channel?}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5927         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} packet\_idx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5928 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5929         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (packet\_idx = 0; packet\_idx < num\_packets; ++packet\_idx) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5930             stbi\_\_pic\_packet *packet = \&packets[packet\_idx];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5931             stbi\_uc *dest = result + y*width * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5932 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5933             \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (packet-\/>type) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{5936 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5937             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 0: \{\textcolor{comment}{//uncompressed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5938                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x;}

\DoxyCodeLine{5940                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (x = 0; x<width; ++x, dest += 4)}

\DoxyCodeLine{5942                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5943                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5944             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5945 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5946             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 1:\textcolor{comment}{//Pure RLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5947             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5948                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} left = width, i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5949 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5950                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (left>0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5951                     stbi\_uc count, value[4];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5952 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5953                     count = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5954                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_at\_eof(s))   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad file"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}file too short (pure read count)"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5955 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5956                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (count > left)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5957                         count = (stbi\_uc)left;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5958 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5959                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_readval(s, packet-\/>channel, value))  \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5960 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5961                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i<count; ++i, dest += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5962                         stbi\_\_copyval(packet-\/>channel, dest, value);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5963                     left -\/= count;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5964                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5965             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5966             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5967 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5968             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 2: \{\textcolor{comment}{//Mixed RLE}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6482 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_hdr\_convert(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float} *output, stbi\_uc *input, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp)}

\DoxyCodeLine{6484     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (input[3] != 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6485         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6486         \textcolor{comment}{// Exponent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6487         f1 = (float)ldexp(1.0f, input[3] -\/ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})(128 + 8));}
\DoxyCodeLine{6488         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp <= 2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6489             output[0] = (input[0] + input[1] + input[2]) * f1 / 3;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6491             output[0] = input[0] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6492             output[1] = input[1] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6493             output[2] = input[2] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6494         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6495         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp == 2) output[1] = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6496         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp == 4) output[3] = 1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6502             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}

\DoxyCodeLine{6504         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 1: output[0] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6505             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6506         \}}
